msg:Traveling to Wuzhen this spring, we stayed at the Midnight Hotel (the name of the hotel is obviously taken from the novel "Midnight" by the writer Mao Dun, because Mao Dun is from Wuzhen). We stayed for 2 nights and had a great experience. First, the hotel is in a good location. Opposite is the Dongzha Scenic Area, which is only a step away. When going to Xizha, the hotel has a free shuttle bus that departs every half hour, which is very convenient. The hotel also provides free sightseeing buses in the scenic area.
Second, the hotel caters well. It offers a set meal of only 168 yuan, with 6 dishes, which is enough for a family of four, and it is very delicious, especially the salt-baked white water fish, special sauce-flavored duck and sister-in-law‚Äôs tofu. My friend After eating it, I was full of praise. Breakfast is buffet style and very rich. Compared with those who spend 300 to 500 yuan per person on meals at scenic spots, this hotel can be called a conscientious enterprise.
Third, many details are admirable.
‚Äî‚ÄîRed serving chopsticks. We are accustomed to using serving chopsticks when dining out. Although most hotels provide them, they are of the same color, so it is easy to get confused when eating. The serving chopsticks in Midnight Hotel are red, so there is no mistake.
‚Äî‚ÄîA toilet seat in the bathroom. For guests who are a bit mysophobic or particularly particular, this move must be appreciated.
‚Äî‚ÄîBooks in the guest room. For book lovers, the books displayed in the room are like meeting old friends in a foreign country. Although there are not many books, they have a common theme, which is to introduce all aspects of Wuzhen so that you can have an in-depth understanding of Wuzhen's history and culture through the scenery when traveling.
‚Äî‚ÄîThe TV has a playback function. The hotels we stayed in ranged from luxurious to simple, and there were quite a lot of them. The TVs rarely played back the TV sets. During the trip, I often felt regretful that I couldn't watch my favorite programs. It was really surprising to find that the TV set in the Midnight Hotel could make up for this regret!
Fourth, the hotel has a good service attitude.
Special thanks to the waiters Ms. Liu and Manager Zhou for their considerate service.
I won‚Äôt introduce details like this one by one. I strongly recommend tourists to experience it by themselves. We will choose Midnight again when we come to Wuzhen.
